OMRI Products List
Crop Products
   
                         1
 
OMRI has determined the following products 
are allowed for use in accordance with 
National Organic Program (NOP) standards, 
for the use indicated and in keeping with any 
applicable use restrictions as specified. 
Producers should consult with their USDA-
accredited certifying body before using any 
new products. Updated February 10, 2022.
